Enjoyed our dinner at this place. The nachos were strong and the tacos were delicious. The service was very attentive and the owner or manager visited with us a few different times to ensure we we're satisfied.
The only criticism was the ambiance, or lack thereof. The lighting was quite dim and the seating a bit uncomfortable. Hopefully they can address some of these minor items.< /Text>

I visit dba256 pretty often, whenever I'm in the mood for a beer and live music. The venue acts as an art gallery as well, so the walls are always changing with new pieces from what I assume are local artists. The music varies depending on the night with weekends featuring local rock bands and djs. The beer list is great with rotating handles and fair prices. The vibe of the place is relaxes, so I always like stopping by and enjoying the scene.< /Review>

< text>
Ok, so first and foremost, New Era had the best payout on recycled material. If that isn't enough, they regularly have coupons for even higher payouts (current coupon gets you $2.00 per lb for cans) in "The Shopper" booklets found for Free at markets and liquor stores around town.

Recycling yards are, in general, a little messy due to the nature of the business. New Era maintains a clear area, and they staff the recycling center with friendly individuals that are quick to answer questions and off assistance.

If you aren't going to New Era Metals, you are passing up the best recycling yard around!!</text>

< time>
1526975582277</time>
< Text>
They may call this a "used" car showroom but it is far more than that.  The exterior is plainly industrial so the facade understates the great content that lies within. I am telling you to hold your breath when you enter this building if you love fantastic automobiles because it will take your breath away over and over...

My experience, I walked into the showroom last week and was literally stunned by what I found. The front area (three lavish rooms), it is like a country club lounge and an auto museum combined... Pool table, large screen television, lounge tables, sofas, and more are all available to the public. This is a very special sleek environment that has that classy feel one would naturally associate with the top level product that Crevier is known to offer.

Walking through the lounge into the spacious showroom that is large enough to be an airline hanger I gaze long afield to see rows and rows of amazing cars. Classics that are in practically perfect condition.. all of them!

I had met a member who pointed me towards his pride, a 2013 Boss 302 (500hp) SchoolBus Yellow Mustang.. For sure one of the newer offerings but wow, it is gorgeous!

I asked a visiting group which car was the favorite. One in the party immediately pointed to a1936 Cord that is spectacular. He told me that he preferred a 1937 model but this beauty would stand in it's absence, no hesitation on his part.

Meanwhile, I hear the gutteral sounds of a carefully driven Grey Ferrari that was being looked at.. I then talked with the man they have cleaning and waxing all these gorgeous cars (I found out his favorite wax and also why he chooses that particular product). I asked a group that is from Port Hueneme, California which car they would pick if they could have any... The gal in this threesome told me, "The Pink Hollywood Jeep"... She pointed it out towards the back of the showroom (see my photos.. she said it was in a movie).

Some members have their classic car in the Crevier Showroom because they enjoy sharing it with others; people that come through the showroom are delighted by the collection.

Many of these gorgeous historical classic cars are for sale so this is a great place to find that polished and pampered classic that you have been searching for (they have a list if you are interested).

A great place to visit when you are in Costa Mesa. You will love Crevier Classic Cars!

By:
cmilton111 (Charles Milton)
Google Guide
5.20.2018</Text>
